<Text>I used to wait here for a while every week when my son had a work related injury, and was seeing urgent care next door.

Now I miss the excuse.

Smart & Final should be glad these fellows are here -- I look at their flier to see if I have a reason to go there and to Namaste (other S Asian grocers are closer to home).

< Review>
As a fist time mommy my daughter Catalina was having issues breast feeding when she was born. I decided to seek help from a lactation consultant that later suggested I have my daughter evaluated for a lip and tounge tie. We were referred to Irvine Children's Dentistry where Dr. Yvonne evaluated my 6 week-old baby. She was very gentle with her and diagnosed her with both a lip and tongue tie. Dr. Yvonne advised for her to have a frenectomy in order for my baby to properly latch and nurse. She was very thorough in explaining the procedure, after care exercises and ensuring that Catalina was comfortable before, during and after the procedure. All of our questions were answered (and yes I had A LOT of questions!). I was very nervous going into her appointment but after speaking to Dr. Yvonne I knew my daughter was in good hands. From the moment we were warmly greeted by Jose at front desk, we knew that we had made the right choice coming here. Thank you to all of the wonderful staff for being so supportive and caring for my daughter. My daughter has made amazing improvement in nursing after her frenectomy. As a mother, I highly recommend Irvine Children's Dentistry to all parents.<//Review>

< Review>
My boys have been coming here for almost 3yrs. The staff is super friendly and do a great job with the kids, by making them feel special. My youngest overcame his fear of the "tooth Dr" after his second visit. The staff made him feel very comfortable at this dentistry.

My oldest is in the process of getting a device in his mouth, I regret not remembering the proper name for it, so forgive me. The device is to bring his jaw forward, that will eventually aligne his mouth together. My son ran out of seprators (small ruberbands used to space out the teeth, that will allow the device to go on smoothly) and used my elastics in substitute of the separators.

Nice try being creative, but epic fail. So, don't try substituting anything for the sperators as I did. The elastics held on at first but because the we're clear it blended with his teeth and gum and was hard to find. The elastic used as a separator slipped all the way down to the button of his gum and wedged tightly between both the gum and tooth. The lady that attended my son listed to his complaints. Although it was impossible to find the elastic, she managed to fish it out. Literally speaking, with her spesias orthodontist tools .

Thank you, Sandra RDA in Irvine, CA! If you for being so dedicated to the children and for listening to them. I can't imagine what pain or infection he could have gotten if the band was left in his tooth. Millions of thank yous!!!!

You'll need to give this place an opportunity, your children won't regret it!<//Review>

<review>Great Facility for Family Fun and for Individualized workouts!
No matter the weather the C.V. Starr is a place to be physically active! This place has a two giant swimming pools, one for leisure, and one for competitive/exercise. It also has a water slide and a lazy river! & that's not all! It also has three different workout rooms two for classes (like zumba, yoga, spin, etc...) and another one large room containing exercise machines and other equipment. This place also has two more event rooms that can be combined for large meetings or parties or can be separated for smaller parties like birthday parties. Each room when used for birthday parties comes with free entrance to swimming for your guests! Oh and I almost forgot, the C.V. Starr also has creative classes like; tapestry arts, robotics, digital media fun, gymnastics, music, and much more...
Individuals looking for a workout, to learn something new, to connect with others, or for aquatic fun will love the C.V. Starr community Center.</review>< Pics>

< text>
This is easily the best indoor pool facility and community center in northern California. With a lazy river , awesome slides and many diving boards among several pools and spas , this little secret in the middle of Fort Bragg California is not to be missed . Not only do they have top notch water activities available but they also have a skate/bike park , bocce ball , horse shoe pits and volleyball courts as well as showers , lockers , ample parking and very reasonable rates.</text>

< Text>
If it wasn't for the fact that C.V. Starr grew up in Fort Bragg, I don't know that this place would ever exist. A huge heated swimming pool with areas for kids and adults, workout rooms, weight lifting. And it's affordable for just about anyone. There's also a skatepark out back, and a dog park in front. One of the true gems of Fort Bragg.
They also offer very affordable swim classes for kids, and room rentals with pool access for birthday parties, etc.< /Text>

The trail goes down to beach is pretty short, our 3 years old toddler handled it without problem. Tide pool area is very enjoyable. Public restroom near golf car return area is still available in COVID lockdown time, which a great plus for the little ones.<//Text>

<user_id>118416870583115163935< /user_id><Name>joyce w< /Name>< Time>
1551612131248<//Time>
<Rating>5</Rating>< review>
Beautifully kept "park" with picnic tables along the edges within the golf course. Great place for picnics or to enjoy the weather. Be warned, there isn't much shade though.
The main paved path in the park takes you on a loop. It does connect to several trails that lead down to the ocean. For steep switchbacks, take the dirt trail that starts on the far side (ocean side) of the paved path. For an easier hike down, a wide dirt path extends toward the golf course (away from the clubhouse) with a smaller path coming off of it. You can also follow the wide path around the golf course-a couple other hiking trails extend down to the rocky beach from this. Some are more difficult than others.<//review>

< text>
This place is an AMAZING find. I wish there was one closer to my home. I could go here every day because they have so many different HEALTHY choices. Healthy, delicious and FRESH food at decent prices COOKED ONCE ORDERED! That's right,  it's fresh,  so if you order any kind of meat,  make sure you give yourself enough time to wait for meat to cook which takes time. While sitting at lunch, and I usually go a couple times a week,  I've witnessed a few people get frustrated because their food takes longer than it would at McDonalds. Tammi  recommended I order ahead. So,  now I order ahead of time and my food is ready when I get there to sit down and eat. Thanks Tammi! If you can't order ahead,  bring a friend/co-worker to talk to or pull out your phone and play away while your DELICIOUS meal is being prepared.  Oh yah, I almost forgot.  The staff here is amazing and all very friendly so don't take your anger out on them because you can't be patient and wait for your food. If you have read this far, you gotta try LETTUCE TOSS IT!!</text>

1569679917007< /date>
< rate>
5</rate>
< text>
This is a gorgeous road. It stretches from Lee Vining to the west on a pass which goes all the way to Yosemite.  There are lakes and creeks and the best time to take photos is during fall or first snow.

The road is very windy and steep so take it slow.  During this time of year (not sure if this is all times) you will be required to stop and pay I believe $35 per car at the 12 mile mark.

The drive however for those 12 miles is worth it.  You can turn around and not pay.

I highly recommend taking this pass if you are up at the Mammoth Lakes area or Mono Lake.

We didn't have much time, so we only took a few photos, but there are so many cool places to check out.  Totally cool drive!<//text>

< review>
Gorgeous decor and amazing service at this new establishment inside Universal Citywalk. We decided to try this place for lunch before we went to Universal Studios horror nights. We ordered:

Pomodoro - light and fresh
Chicken fettuccine - good but under-seasoned. I added salt and chili peppers to it.
Margherita pizza - thick crust with thinner middle. Delicious though!
Lasagna x 2 - we all agreed that this was the worst dish. The lasagna tasted really soggy and bland. Did not taste fresh.
A round of Peroni Italian beer - so crisp and light!

I love that they give you a sourdough boule for the table. It's so cute! For my husband's birthday, he received a complimentary tiramisu which was freshly made and a nice way to end our meal. For 4 people, we were so stuffed that it took a couple of hours of walking around in Universal Studios to feel normal again! Next time, we'll order 1 less entree.

Service was impeccable! Overall, a good experience despite the lasagna. Considering the decor, service, and food, this really is the best restaurant in Universal Citywalk. Also, lunch prices were so reasonable, I was shocked!< /review>

I came here for lunch and while the outdoor patio has a really nice atmosphere, the food leaves something to be desired. I saw squid ink pasta on the photos on yelp but didn't find it on the menu, so I asked our server if they still had it and he let me know that it was on the dinner menu but they could serve it for lunch as well. < Review>
Vivo Italian Kitchen is a fine dining Italian establishment that serves mains, pastas, salads and pizza. We had a family trip there including locals and out of towners and for the most part we all enjoyed what we ordered.

My wife especially appreciated that they had gluten free pasta available which she thought was good, though the side of broccoli she ordered was a bit over cooked. (You need a little bit of crunch left in your vegetables.)

I had the Margherita Pizza made with fresh mozzarella and ‚Äúgrandma‚Äôs sauce‚Äù which was described by our waiter as made with more spices than regular marinara. In practice the pizza was good but I didn‚Äôt notice anything extra flavorful about the sauce and I‚Äôm wondering if our waiter didn‚Äôt have the best answer to my question. There was plenty of sauce though, which I always appreciate as many pizza joints get kind of skimpy on their pies, and the pizza was cooked perfectly with a nice, crispy, thin crust and the cheese perfectly cooked (with those little brown spots), not underdone as often happens with pizzas and fresh mozzarella.

I also enjoyed the red blend wine I ordered.

Their bread service was good too. It‚Äôs served with an olive oil / sun-dried tomato tapenade, and also with butter ‚Äì Nice to get both since sometimes you don‚Äôt get butter when you want it.

There‚Äôs a good, well stocked bar and plenty to choose from on the cocktail menu as well.</Review>

Very nice looking place. Great Lobby with tables/seating for eating/watching news/coffee. Rooms have kitchenette, large fridge, microwave, stove, breakfast seating, w/ chairs. Large bathroom with shower/bath, toilet, sink, built in hairdryer. Large bed, pillows TOO soft, comfortable bedding. Recliner in room(ours didn't recline) night stand on 1 side of bed. Flat screen TV w movies for rent or you can watch cable TV. Has a linen closet wbehind a closed door- separate from the actual clothing closet which has plenty of drawers, hanging space, luggage storage a curtain to cover closet space. Kitchenette has cabinets above & below. Telephone in room. Rooms are odd on one side & even on other side- bit confusing to find at NIGHT, unless front lobby staff show you WHERE YOUR ROOM IS.<//Text>

<Review>Suddenly planned trip to San jose, only this hotel had rooms available near the office I wanted to go. It was $143+taxes per day for the Deluxe Room. From the reviews I read from net, my expectations were low. It was corporate booking at corporate rate apparently. It was planned for 5 nights.

I reached this place around 8.30 AM on a Sunday morning. I had to wait in their common visitors area for around 30 mins to get the room. Yeap, it was an early check-in. Receptionist was helpful and managed to get a room cleaned as soon as possible once the housekeeping people were in.

Now comes to rooms :
Room : Room was clean and spacious enough. It had a kitchen area with Induction cook spaces and microwave. But no kitchen utensils! - But I think you get that from the Reception area if needed (not sure though). I am not a cooking person :). Bathroom was spacious enough with a bathtub. Basic stuff like bath soap, shampoo & hair drier are provided. The bath tub water blocker was broken needed repair & one table lamp was not working.

Service : Weekly room service only. You wont get room service if you are staying there for less than a week. So of course I was not eligible for room service. But if you need towels or other stuff you can just go and ask in the reception. I wanted an early check-in by cutting short the stay there by a day. I didn't face any problem they accepted the early check-in & returned the one days rent back to my credit card (5 days charge was taken in advance). It went smooth.

Complimentary breakfast : Its grab & go breakfast. Some packed oats (you can have with hot water - healthy though :) ), sweetened buns (danish pastry kind), oats bars & coffee/tea options.

Internet - Yes. free wifi available. Not high speed though but enough for basic stuffs.

Swimming pool - Not available

See the pics I have attached - to get an idea on how deluxe room looks like.

laundry service : self operated coin-washing machines available.
Suggestions :
- So this will be good for pure vegetarian(from India) people who like to cook there during extended stays
- Good locations, proximity to San jose office
- A chines market & restaurants are at walkable distance

Final verdict : I didn't find this place & service as bad as mentioned in other reviews. $143 + taxes doesn't look that cheap for me but yeah budget option compared to other hotels nearby. I think they have shortage of house keeping people and rooms need a little more maintenance.
So I will rate this average & recommend for people who are budget conscious, long stays, people who wants to cook for themselves during their stay.</Review></record></dataset><record>

<review>I have stayed for several months in all the hotels in the vicinity (Milpitas). This is a very nice and affordable hotel to stay. The price is unbeatable compared to all the hotels in the vicinity (almost 1/2 to 1/3rd less!). Very close to grocery store and various asian restaurants. A 5 min car ride will take you to Bestbuy, Walmart, in & Out, Ross and McCarthy Ranch which has all hotels that you can ask for. The hotel  has  a kitchen in the room which is the best advantage. Your room is cleaned once a week.  High speed internet comes at an extra price.

Positives:
1. A decent size kitchen with 2 burner electric stove, Regrigerator, Kitchen utensils and Microwave.
2. A large size bathroom with bath tub.
3. A table for working. Large size room.
4. Rooms has a TV with lot of channels.
5. The staff (especially Trang in the front desk and Manager Khan ) are very friendly and  very concerned about your stay and comfort. They constantly seek your feedback and work on it.
6. Basic breakfast  if free - muffin, oats, coffee/ tea.
7. The price is very affordable.

Overall i am happy to have chosen this hotel.<//review></record></dataset><record>

<Review>Nice place to stay and had a pleasent stay. Recommended if you cook on your own and want to save on high restaurant bills.

The hotel does not have a restaurant however they do have a complementary breakfast which includes coffee, snack bars , cakes, chocolate etc. These are good to grab and rush to work.

The staff is very proffessional. Room service happens once every week if you are staying longer.

About the facility:

The rooms are clean.
My refrigerator leaked water. The hotel tried to service it initially. Then they replaced it.
There is cooking equipment made available to you if you want to cook in your room. The free internet is sufficient for Skype calls or YouTube streaming. Mcarthy Ranch market is close by for grocery shopping. Laundry rooms are coin operated.<//Review></record>
